
=== Zvfbfa - Additional BF16 vector compute support extension

[[vector-single-width-bfloat-add-subtract]]
==== Vector Single-Width BFloat Add/Subtract Intrinsics

[,c]
----
vbfloat16mf4_t __riscv_vfadd_vv_bf16mf4(vbfloat16mf4_t vs2, vbfloat16mf4_t vs1,
                                        size_t vl);

                                        size_t vl);

[[vector-single-width-bfloat-multiply]]
==== Vector Single-Width BFloat Multiply Intrinsics

[,c]
----
vbfloat16mf4_t __riscv_vfmul_vv_bf16mf4(vbfloat16mf4_t vs2, vbfloat16mf4_t vs1,
                                        size_t vl);
vbfloat16mf4_t __riscv_vfmul_vf_bf16mf4(vbfloat16mf4_t vs2, __bf16 rs1,
                                        size_t vl);
vbfloat16mf2_t __riscv_vfmul_vv_bf16mf2(vbfloat16mf2_t vs2, vbfloat16mf2_t vs1,
                                        size_t vl);
vbfloat16mf2_t __riscv_vfmul_vf_bf16mf2(vbfloat16mf2_t vs2, __bf16 rs1,
                                        size_t vl);
vbfloat16m1_t __riscv_vfmul_vv_bf16m1(vbfloat16m1_t vs2, vbfloat16m1_t vs1,
                                      size_t vl);
vbfloat16m1_t __riscv_vfmul_vf_bf16m1(vbfloat16m1_t vs2, __bf16 rs1, size_t vl);
vbfloat16m2_t __riscv_vfmul_vv_bf16m2(vbfloat16m2_t vs2, vbfloat16m2_t vs1,
                                      size_t vl);
vbfloat16m2_t __riscv_vfmul_vf_bf16m2(vbfloat16m2_t vs2, __bf16 rs1, size_t vl);
vbfloat16m4_t __riscv_vfmul_vv_bf16m4(vbfloat16m4_t vs2, vbfloat16m4_t vs1,
                                      size_t vl);
vbfloat16m4_t __riscv_vfmul_vf_bf16m4(vbfloat16m4_t vs2, __bf16 rs1, size_t vl);
vbfloat16m8_t __riscv_vfmul_vv_bf16m8(vbfloat16m8_t vs2, vbfloat16m8_t vs1,
                                      size_t vl);
vbfloat16m8_t __riscv_vfmul_vf_bf16m8(vbfloat16m8_t vs2, __bf16 rs1, size_t vl);
// masked functions
